Director Jon Watts wanted the goggles on the black Spider-Man costume to be the exact opposite of something that Iron Man would wear. They were also inspired by a popular style of flip-up glasses from the 1980s.  This is the first live-action appearance of Mysterio.  The first Spider-Man film where the Sony Columbia Pictures logo has its traditional music instead of a musical score over it. I think that there is more than one Spiderman in the MCU as there are far too many inconsistencies with all Spiderman films.   Tobey Spiderman.  Out of all the Spidermen, he is the only one who doesn't use web tech as his web swinging abilities are a biological mutation from being bitten from an engineered spider.  In his reality, Norman Osborn was working on glider tech for the military.  However, due to overwhelming pressure to deliver, he took a huge risk and experimented on himself which resulted in him becoming crazy thus becoming The Green Goblin.  Harvey Osborn who was Peter's best friend wanted to get revenge on him for killing his father, thus he became the new Green Goblin.   Andrew Spiderman:  Unlike Tobey's Spiderman his love interest was Gwen Stacy rather than MJ.  It was revealed in his reality that his father had incorporated his own DNA into the engineered spiders as a means to prevent others from abusing it's power.  This is why Andrew Spiderman's abilities were able to "take."   Norman Osborn in this reality didn't become the Green Goblin, but instead died from a genetic disease (I forget what it was called).  Harry learned that this disease is hereditary and therefore desperately searched for a cure.  In his desperation he had himself injected with spider serum which didn't "take" due to incompatibility.  As a result he had suffered nasty side effects which was managed by the regenerative capabilities of the Goblin suit.  He also wanted to get revenge on peter, however his motivation for vengeance was based on the fact that Spiderman refused to give him his blood to help cure Harry.   Tom Spiderman:  In this version his romantic interest was also MJ except she is black.  Also his best friend is Ned not Harry.  And unlike the other versions of Spiderman he was the only one that met Tony Stark and became an Avenger.   Now one might assume that the films with Tobey and Andrew are not canon and therefore can be ignored.  I don't believe however that is the case as the concept of the multiverse was deliberately mention in this trailer.  We know from the previous films that most of the villains had died and yet somehow that have returned. Therefore I believe that all the villains were from the alternate realities from the previous films.  If this is the case, then that begs the question:  When in the timeline did the villains get brought to Tom Spiderman's reality?  If any of the villains were fighting with the alternate Spidermen when they were transported to a different reality, then it is likely Tobey and Andrew Spiderman would also have been sucked into Tom Spiderman's reality.  Which I think it is necessary for the story as I think that despite Tom Spiderman having an advance Spider suit, he would get his butt whooped pretty bad without assistance.  Yes I know there is also Dr Strange, but even then it might not be enough. So in conclusion, I think that each of the previous films were alternate versions of Spiderman and that there is a good chance that Tobey Maguire and Andrew Garfield will make an appearance to help fight against the combined formidable strength of their adversaries.

2:45 that's not Murdock - in the clip immediately before the one shown dude is walking (likely into the interrogation room) with his arms crossed and no cane assisting him. This being in a public setting, I doubt Matt would walk around like that.
Calling it now 2 villains for each spiderman.... Vulture and scorpion (Holland) goblin and Dr ock (Tobey) lizard and electro(Garfield) will make the sinister 6.

So the sinister six are coming, loki is trying to find sylvie, Kang is coming, the multiverse is starting to open, wanda is going to destroy half the universe to find her children, barren mordo will come back for revenge, Shuma gorath and Dormamu's niece are rumored to be in Multiverse of Madness and celestials are about to deal with the fate of the planet. And strange is on a winter vacation in his sanatorium:)
